This is an archive containing the FPGA Editor for Atmel's 6000 FPGA series, the Lola hardware description language compiler, and the design checker to check an FPGA-layout against a specification written in Lola.

This release is compiled for
Oberon for Windows(TM)  V4.0-1.41 (July 8 1995)

For further information and documentation, please refer to
http://www-cs.ethz.ch/~ludwig

Installation Instructions

First click with the middle mouse button or the Ctrl key on the keyboard on the command AsciiCoder.DecodeFiles below. Then, click on the System.Open command. In the AT.Tool, there is an example section, where you can find example designs testing out the FPGA on the AT-board. If you have problems with the board, change its base address with the DIP switches on the board and change the address used by the loader in the AT.Configuration.Text (see AT.Tool at the end).

If you have problems with this software, please write us!

Stefan H.-M. Ludwig	Stephan W. Gehring	October 1995
ludwig@inf.ethz.ch	gehring@inf.ethz.ch

System.Open AT.Tool
